I never knew it was a rebuild of the original "alien encounter" and thought the black out part of it was the best part of it. It was surreal for sure, though I guess if it was still around, it wouldn't have the same experience as other rides would. Shame to know it's been called the worst, but I guess Disney will always find a way to build off of failures for something bigger in the future (maybe).

For some random context:  This area was originally host to â€œextra-terrorestrial alien encounterâ€ which was basically a pitch black sensory horror experience. Its a circular room with a big alien animatronic in a cage in the center and when the monster â€œbroke outâ€ the lights would go out. Then the chairs you sit in would play audio and shake around and stuff to simulate the alien crawling around the room on top of your chair. It was closed because it was too scary or something so they opened this, which was identical in premise but more comedy instead of horror. People still hated it, so it shut down. The theaters are now just backrooms used for storage and all the robots (the stitch one and a few more in the queue line) were all presumably scrapped for parts.  Or they could still be rotting away in there. Who knows.

Fnaf Disney be like
A Springlock suit is a special animatronic that can be used as both an animatronic and suit. In order to turn the animatronic into "suit mode", you will require a special crank which pushes the endoskeleton and mechanical gears to the sides of the suit, making just enough space to wedge a person inside. The two most notable springlock suits are Spring Bonnie and Fredbear.  The suits contain a metal endoskeleton which has a line from the head to the groin and legs. Once it has been wound up using a metal crank, the suit splits vertically in half, allowing a person to wedge themselves inside and wear it. If the gears of the suit get damaged or damp, the endoskeleton snaps back together, crushing the person inside instantly.

It was actually just a re-skinned attraction. It used to be Alien Encounter, which was supposed to have the Alien movie monster. They couldn't get the licensing so they created their own monster, and it featured a similar plot to the Stitch one (being trapped in the tube, escaping, lights going off, smells, the seat vibrating). The difference was Alien Encounter was a horror ride and the NPC characters that showed up were killed by the creature and it was more creepy. It flopped hard because parents were pissed about it being too scary.
